# Stage 1 code review — ml-service MiewID preprocessing switch

Codex review request for the implementation of design item 1
(ml-service preprocessing torchvision → albumentations).

## Context

Repo: `/mnt/c/ml-service`. Branch: working tree (no commit yet).

Design was reviewed by you in round 1 (`docs/plans/2026-05-19-parity-fix-design-review.md` in the Wildbook repo). Your findings folded into this implementation:
- Used `MiewidModel.IMAGE_SIZE` class constant (#4).
- Imported `albumentations` directly (not lazy) since it's already a hard dep at `requirements.txt:24` (#5).
- Updated BOTH preprocess sites — `app/models/miewid.py` AND `app/routers/explain_router.py:35-46` for PairX (#3).
- Did NOT add an autocast change (#3 → defer).
- No SQL migration of stored `MATCHRESULTPROSPECT.SCORE` (#1 → regen on test deploy instead).

## Validation already performed

Ran `/tmp/extraction_parity_test.py` end-to-end with the patched code. Result table (cosine between every variant pair):

```
A (ml-service patched)              vs B (WBIA as-is, autocast)      1.0000000000
A vs C (WBIA preprocess, FP32 only)                                  1.0000000000
A vs D (WBIA preprocess + PIL crop)                                  1.0000000000
A vs E (mls preprocess + cv2 crop)                                   1.0000000000
B vs C (autocast on/off)                                             1.0000000000
D vs A (only transform library differs)                              1.0000000000
E vs A (only crop algorithm differs)                                 1.0000000000
```

Bit-identical embeddings across every variant. ||e|| also matches (58.7148 on both sides). On CPU autocast is a no-op; the script was run on CPU.

## Review scope

1. Is the `albumentations.Compose([Resize, Normalize, ToTensorV2])` chain
   in `miewid.py` SEMANTICALLY identical to wbia-plugin-miew-id's
   `get_valid_transforms` at `wbia_miew_id/datasets/transforms.py:68-75`?
   The local test confirms numerical parity at the embedding level, so
   the answer is empirically yes — but worth a static-code-review pass.
2. The `process_image` flow in `extract_embeddings` upstream of the
   preprocess call still converts to PIL via `Image.open(...).convert('RGB')`.
   The crop+rotate path also stays PIL. We then `np.array(...)` at the
   preprocess call. Any concern about the round-trip vs going numpy from
   the start? My read: PIL→numpy at the boundary is fine and matches
   what `Image.fromarray + transforms.ToTensor` was doing internally.
3. The `explain_router.preprocess` change drops the `Image.fromarray(...)`
   wrap (caller already has numpy from cv2). Correct?
4. `torchvision.transforms as transforms` is still imported in
   `explain_router.py` — used at `process_image` line 127 for the
   `transforms.Resize(img_size)(Image.fromarray(image))` chip resize for
   visualization display. Out of scope but worth flagging — could be left
   torchvision (display-only) or migrated for consistency (no parity impact
   either way).
5. Is `ToTensorV2()` without explicit `p=1.0` correct? Default is `p=1.0`.
6. Anything else.

**Read-only review. Do not modify any files.**

     1	from .base_model import BaseModel
     2	import logging
     3	from transformers import AutoModel

     5	from typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional, Tuple
     6	import timm
     7	import torch
     8	import torch.nn as nn
     9	import albumentations
    10	from albumentations.pytorch import ToTensorV2
    11	# torchvision import removed: preprocessing now uses albumentations to match
    12	# wbia-plugin-miew-id's training/inference pipeline. See the comment on
    13	# self.preprocess below for details.
    14	from PIL import Image
    15	import numpy as np
    16	import io
    17	import math
    18	from app.utils.checkpoint_utils import get_checkpoint_path
    19	
    20	logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    21	
    22	
    23	class GeM(nn.Module):
    24	    """Generalized Mean Pooling."""
    25	    def __init__(self, p=3, eps=1e-6):
    26	        super().__init__()
    27	        self.p = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(1) * p)
    28	        self.eps = eps
    29	
    30	    def forward(self, x):
    31	        return nn.functional.avg_pool2d(
    32	            x.clamp(min=self.eps).pow(self.p),
    33	            (x.size(-2), x.size(-1))
    34	        ).pow(1.0 / self.p)
    35	
    36	
    37	class MiewIdNet(nn.Module):
    38	    """Standalone MiewID model architecture matching wbia-plugin-miew-id training code."""
    39	    def __init__(self, model_name='efficientnetv2_rw_m'):
    40	        super().__init__()
    41	        self.backbone = timm.create_model(model_name, pretrained=False)
    42	        final_in_features = self.backbone.classifier.in_features
    43	        self.backbone.classifier = nn.Identity()
    44	        self.backbone.global_pool = nn.Identity()
    45	        self.pooling = GeM()
    46	        self.bn = nn.BatchNorm1d(final_in_features)
    47	
    48	    def forward(self, x):
    49	        x = self.backbone.forward_features(x)
    50	        x = self.pooling(x).view(x.size(0), -1)
    51	        return self.bn(x)
    52	
    53	
    54	class MiewidModel(BaseModel):
    55	    # Input shape the MiewID v3/v4 architecture expects. Also the shape used
    56	    # at training time by wbia-plugin-miew-id (see
    57	    # wbia_miew_id/datasets/transforms.py:get_valid_transforms). Kept as a
    58	    # class-level constant so the preprocessing config and any future
    59	    # model_info reporting stay in sync.
    60	    IMAGE_SIZE = (440, 440)
    61	
    62	    def __init__(self):
    63	        self.model = None
    64	        self.model_info = {}
    65	        self.device = "cuda"
    66	        self.preprocess = None
    67	        self.use_checkpoint = False
    68	
    69	    def load(self, model_path: str = "", device: str = "cuda", **kwargs) -> None:
    70	        self.device = device
    71	        checkpoint_path = kwargs.get('checkpoint_path')
    72	        
    73	        # Check if we should use checkpoint loading
    74	        if checkpoint_path:
    75	            self.use_checkpoint = True
    76	            local_checkpoint_path = get_checkpoint_path(checkpoint_path)
    77	            # Remove checkpoint_path from kwargs to avoid duplicate parameter error
    78	            filtered_kwargs = {k: v for k, v in kwargs.items() if k != 'checkpoint_path'}
    79	            version = kwargs.get('version', 3)
    80	            if isinstance(version, (int, float)) and version >= 4:
    81	                self._load_standalone(local_checkpoint_path, device)
    82	            else:
    83	                self._load_from_checkpoint(local_checkpoint_path, device, **filtered_kwargs)
    84	        else:
    85	            self.use_checkpoint = False
    86	            self._load_from_huggingface(device, **kwargs)
    87	
    88	        # Initialize preprocessing transforms.
    89	        # Matches wbia-plugin-miew-id's get_valid_transforms exactly so
    90	        # embeddings extracted here agree numerically with embeddings
    91	        # extracted by the legacy WBIA MiewID pipeline for the same input
    92	        # image+bbox. albumentations 1.3.1's Normalize defaults are ImageNet
    93	        # mean/std with max_pixel_value=255.0, equivalent to torchvision's
    94	        # ToTensor + Normalize(mean,std) chain modulo the bilinear resize
    95	        # implementation (PIL vs cv2.INTER_LINEAR) — and the model was
    96	        # trained against cv2 bilinear, so albumentations is the correct
    97	        # match. Bumping to torchvision was a ~3° angular drift per
    98	        # embedding, large enough to reshuffle top-N matches.
    99	        self.preprocess = albumentations.Compose([
   100	            albumentations.Resize(*self.IMAGE_SIZE),
   101	            albumentations.Normalize(),
   102	            ToTensorV2(),
   103	        ])
   104	
   105	        self.model_info = {
   106	            'model_type': 'miewid',
   107	            'device': device,
   108	            'imgsz': kwargs.get('imgsz', 440),
   109	            'version': kwargs.get('version', 3),
   110	            'checkpoint_path': checkpoint_path,
   111	            'use_checkpoint': self.use_checkpoint
   112	        }
   113	
   114	    def _load_from_huggingface(self, device: str, **kwargs) -> None:
   115	        """Load model from HuggingFace Hub."""
   116	        if kwargs.get('version', 3) == 3:
   117	            model_tag = f"conservationxlabs/miewid-msv3"
   118	        else:
   119	            model_tag = f"conservationxlabs/miewid-msv2"
   120	            
   121	        self.model = AutoModel.from_pretrained(model_tag, trust_remote_code=True)
   122	        self.model.eval()
   123	        self.model.to(device)
   124	        logger.info(f"Loaded MiewID model from HuggingFace: {model_tag}")
   125	
   126	    def _apply_checkpoint(self, model: nn.Module, checkpoint_path: str, device: str, strict: bool = True) -> None:
   127	        """Load checkpoint weights into a model and move to device."""
   128	        try:
   129	            checkpoint = torch.load(checkpoint_path, map_location='cpu', weights_only=True)
   130	            model.load_state_dict(checkpoint, strict=strict)
   131	            model.eval()
   132	            model.to(device)
   133	            try:
   134	                model.device = torch.device(device)
   135	            except AttributeError:
   136	                pass  # HuggingFace models have read-only .device property
   137	            self.model = model
   138	            logger.info(f"Loaded MiewID model from checkpoint: {checkpoint_path}")
   139	        except Exception as e:
   140	            logger.error(f"Failed to load checkpoint from {checkpoint_path}: {str(e)}")
   141	            raise HTTPException(
   142	                status_code=500,
   143	                detail=f"Failed to load model checkpoint: {str(e)}"
   144	            )
   145	
   146	    def _load_from_checkpoint(self, checkpoint_path: str, device: str, **kwargs) -> None:
   147	        """Load HuggingFace base model and overlay checkpoint weights."""
   148	        if kwargs.get('version', 3) == 3:
   149	            model_tag = "conservationxlabs/miewid-msv3"
   150	        else:
   151	            model_tag = "conservationxlabs/miewid-msv2"
   152	        model = AutoModel.from_pretrained(model_tag, trust_remote_code=True)
   153	        self._apply_checkpoint(model, checkpoint_path, device, strict=False)
   154	
   155	    def _load_standalone(self, checkpoint_path: str, device: str) -> None:
   156	        """Load model from checkpoint using standalone timm-based architecture."""
   157	        model = MiewIdNet()
   158	        self._apply_checkpoint(model, checkpoint_path, device, strict=True)
   159	
   160	    def get_model_info(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
   161	        """Get information about the loaded model."""
   162	        return self.model_info
   163	    
   164	    def predict(self, **kwargs):
   165	        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"MiewID should not be used for prediction")
   166	
   167	    def crop_and_rotate_image(self, image: Image.Image, bbox: Tuple[int, int, int, int], theta: float = 0.0) -> Image.Image:
   168	        """
   169	        Crop and rotate an image based on bounding box and rotation angle.
   170	        
   171	        Args:
   172	            image: PIL Image
   173	            bbox: Tuple of (x, y, width, height)
   174	            theta: Rotation angle in radians
   175	            
   176	        Returns:
   177	            Cropped and rotated PIL Image
   178	        """
   179	        x, y, w, h = bbox
   180	        
   181	        # Crop the image
   182	        cropped = image.crop((x, y, x + w, y + h))
   183	        
   184	        # Rotate if theta is provided
   185	        if theta != 0.0:
   186	            # Convert radians to degrees
   187	            angle_degrees = math.degrees(theta)
   188	            cropped = cropped.rotate(-angle_degrees, expand=True)
   189	        
   190	        return cropped
   191	
   192	    def extract_embeddings(self, image_bytes: bytes, bbox: Optional[Tuple[int, int, int, int]] = None, theta: float = 0.0) -> np.ndarray:
   193	        """
   194	        Extract embeddings from an image using optional bounding box and rotation.
   195	        
   196	        Args:
   197	            image_bytes: Image data as bytes
   198	            bbox: Optional tuple of (x, y, width, height). If None, uses full image
   199	            theta: Rotation angle in radians
   200	            
   201	        Returns:
   202	            Numpy array containing the embeddings
   203	        """
   204	        try:
   205	            # Load image from bytes
   206	            image = Image.open(io.BytesIO(image_bytes)).convert('RGB')
   207	            
   208	            # Process the image (crop and rotate if bbox provided, otherwise just rotate)
   209	            if bbox is not None:
   210	                processed_image = self.crop_and_rotate_image(image, bbox, theta)
   211	            else:
   212	                # Use full image, only apply rotation if needed
   213	                if theta != 0.0:
   214	                    angle_degrees = math.degrees(theta)
   215	                    processed_image = image.rotate(-angle_degrees, expand=True)
   216	                else:
   217	                    processed_image = image
   218	            
   219	            # Apply preprocessing transforms. albumentations takes numpy HWC RGB;
   220	            # processed_image is a PIL.Image with mode='RGB' from line 185
   221	            # so np.array(...) gives the expected shape and dtype.
   222	            augmented = self.preprocess(image=np.array(processed_image))
   223	            input_tensor = augmented["image"]
   224	            input_batch = input_tensor.unsqueeze(0).to(self.device)
   225	            
   226	            # Extract embeddings
   227	            with torch.no_grad():
   228	                embeddings = self.model(input_batch)
   229	            
   230	            # Convert to numpy and return
   231	            return embeddings.cpu().numpy()
   232	            
   233	        except Exception as e:
   234	            logger.error(f"Error extracting embeddings: {str(e)}")
   235	            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"Error extracting embeddings: {str(e)}")

    30	def is_url(string):
    31	    """Checks if a string is formatted as a url"""
    32	    return string.startswith(('http://', 'https://'))
    33	
    34	async def get_model_handler(request: Request) -> ModelHandler:
    35	    """Dependency to get the model handler from the app state."""
    36	    return request.app.state.model_handler

    38	def preprocess(image, model):
    39	    """Runs preprocessing on an image based on the model to be used."""
    40	    if model.lower().startswith("miewid"):
    41	        # Match wbia-plugin-miew-id's training/inference transforms (and
    42	        # MiewidModel.preprocess) so PairX visualizations operate on the
    43	        # same tensor representation as embedding extraction. albumentations
    44	        # takes a numpy HWC uint8 image; the caller passes a numpy image
    45	        # already, so no PIL round-trip is needed.
    46	        transform = albumentations.Compose([
    47	            albumentations.Resize(*MiewidModel.IMAGE_SIZE),
    48	            albumentations.Normalize(),
    49	            ToTensorV2(),
    50	        ])
    51	        augmented = transform(image=image.astype("uint8"))
    52	        return augmented["image"]
    53	    else:
    54	        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Unsupported model")
    55	
    56	def extend_bb_list(img_list, bb_list):
    57	    """Extends a list a bounding boxes to the length of a list of images.
    58	    Values added mean that no bounding takes place"""
    59	    for x in range(len(img_list) - len(bb_list)):
    60	        bb_list.append([0, 0, 0, 0])
    61	    return bb_list
    62	
    63	def extend_theta_list(img_list, theta_list):
    64	    """Extends a list of thetas to the length of a list of images.
    65	    Thetas added mean that no rotation takes place"""
    66	    for x in range(len(img_list) - len(theta_list)):
    67	        theta_list.append(0.0)
    68	    return theta_list 
    69	
    70	def validate_img_parameters(bbox, theta):
    71	    """Ensure that a bounding box and theta are valid"""
    72	    if len(bbox) != 4:
    73	        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"Each bounding box should have 4 values")
    74	    for x in bbox:
    75	        if x < 0:
    76	            raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Bounding box values should be positive")
    77	
    78	def validate_vis_parameters(body):
    79	    """Checks if body parameters related to a specific visualization algorithm are valid."""
    80	    if body.algorithm.lower() == "pairx":
    81	        if body.k_lines < 0:
    82	            raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"K Lines must be positive")
    83	        if body.k_lines > 99:
    84	            raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"K Lines must be less than 100")
    85	        if body.k_colors < 0:
    86	            raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"K Colors must be positive")
    87	        if body.k_colors > 99:
    88	            raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"K Colors must be less than 100")
    89	        if body.visualization_type not in ["lines_and_colors", "only_lines", "only_colors"]:
    90	            raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Unsupported visualization type.")
    91	        possible_models = ["miewid-msv3", "miewid-msv4.1"]
    92	        if not body.model_id.lower() in possible_models:
    93	            raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Unsupported model for pairx.")
    94	    else:
    95	        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Unsupported algorithm.")
    96	
    97	async def process_image(uri, bbox, theta, crop_bbox, model, device):
    98	    """Reads image in from uri and generates pretransform and transform images to use for visualiztaion. 
    99	    If crop_bbox is true, the preptransform image will be cropped. The transformed image will always be cropped.
   100	    The transformed image will be stored on the device provided, ("cpu", "cuda", etc.)"""
   101	    uri = uri.strip()
   102	    try:
   103	        if is_url(uri):
   104	            async with httpx.AsyncClient() as client:
   105	                response = await client.get(uri)
   106	            if response.status_code != 200:
   107	                raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"Failed to download image: {response.status_code}")
   108	            image_bytes = np.frombuffer(response.content, np.uint8)
   109	            image = cv2.imdecode(image_bytes, cv2.IMREAD_COLOR)
   110	            image = cv2.cvtColor(image, cv2.COLOR_BGR2RGB)
   111	        else:
   112	            path = str(Path(uri).expanduser().resolve())
   113	            image = cv2.imread(path)
   114	            image = cv2.cvtColor(image, cv2.COLOR_BGR2RGB)
   115	    except Exception as e:
   116	        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"Error loading image: {str(e)}")
   117	
   118	    validate_img_parameters(bbox, theta)
   119	
   120	    chip = get_chip_from_img(image, bbox, theta)
   121	    transformed_image = preprocess(chip, model)
   122	    if len(transformed_image.shape) == 3:
   123	            transformed_image = transformed_image.unsqueeze(0)
   124	    if crop_bbox:
   125	        image = chip
   126	    img_size = tuple(transformed_image.shape[-2:])
   127	    image = np.array(transforms.Resize(img_size)(Image.fromarray(image)))
   128	    return image, transformed_image.to(device)
   129	
   130	def process_asyncio_result(result):
   131	    """Processes a result of process_image() when it is run via asyncio."""
   132	    if isinstance(result, Exception):
   133	        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"{str(result)}")
   134	    else:
   135	        image, transform = result
   136	        return image, transform
   137	
   138	def run_pairx(imgs1_transformed, imgs2_transformed, imgs1, imgs2, model, layer_key, 
   139	        k_lines, k_colors, visualization_type):
   140	    """Run PAIR-X on provided images with given parameters.
   141	        
   142	        Args:
   143	            imgs1_transformed: List of transformed images
   144	            imgs2_transformed: List of transformed images. Length should match imgs1_transformed
   145	            imgs1: Untransformed counterparts of imgs1_transformed
   146	            imgs2: Untransformed counterparts of imgs2_transformed
   147	            model: Actual model to be used rather than model id
   148	            layer_key: layer within the model to use for feature matching and relevance propagation. 
   149	                Earlier layer keys lead to visualizations that are focused on very specific points. 
   150	                Later layer keys lead to visualizations that encompass broad swaths of the image.
   151	                Layer keys in the middle tend to be preferred qualitatively.
   152	            k_lines: The number of points on the two images to be matched and connected with lines
   153	                in the visualization. High values of k lines often lead to clearly erroneous matches,
   154	                but do not significantly impact performance.
   155	            k_colors:
   156	                The number of matches to backpropagate relevance on. Higher values of k_colors make 
   157	                the algorithm much slower.
   158	            visualization_type: One of "lines_and_colors", "only_colors", or "only_lines". 
   159	                "lines_and_colors" yields the entire visualization
   160	                "only_colors" crops out the half to only show the backpropagated relevances.
   161	                "only_lines" crops out the bottom half to only show the feature matches.
   162	            
   163	        Returns:
   164	            List of completed visualizations
   165	    """
   166	    
   167	    # There is no reason to do backpropagation if we are not going to display it.
   168	    if visualization_type == "only_lines":
   169	        k_colors = 0
   170	
   171	    if not layer_key in dict(model.named_modules()):
   172	        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Invalid layer key")
   173	
   174	    pairx_imgs = []
   175	    try:
   176	        pairx_imgs = explain(
   177	            torch.cat(imgs1_transformed),
   178	            torch.cat(imgs2_transformed),
   179	            imgs1,
   180	            imgs2,
   181	            model,
   182	            [layer_key],
   183	            k_lines=k_lines,
   184	            k_colors=k_colors,
   185	        )
   186	    # Handle out of memory errors by breaking into two batches and running again
   187	    except Exception as e:
   188	        if str(e).startswith("torch.cuda.OutOfMemoryError:"):
   189	            dim_size = imgs1_transformed.shape[0]
   190	            midpoint = dim_size // 2
   191	            first_half = run_pairx(imgs1_transformed[:midpoint], imgs2_transformed[:midpoint], imgs1[:midpoint], imgs2[:midpoint], model,
   192	                    layer_key, k_lines, k_colors, visualization_type)
   193	            second_half = run_pairx(imgs1_transformed[midpoint:], imgs2_transformed[midpoint:], imgs1[midpoint:], imgs2[midpoint:], model,
   194	                    layer_key, k_lines, k_colors, visualization_type)
   195	            return first_half + second_half
   196	        else:
   197	            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"Internal Server Error")
   198	    finally:
   199	        # PAIR-X backward() accumulates .grad on model params — clear to prevent VRAM growth
   200	        model.zero_grad(set_to_none=True)
   201	    
   202	    toReturn = []
   203	    for pairx_img in pairx_imgs:
   204	        pairx_height = pairx_img.shape[0] // 2
   205	
   206	        if visualization_type == "only_lines":
   207	            pairx_img = pairx_img[:pairx_height]
   208	        elif visualization_type == "only_colors":
   209	            pairx_img = pairx_img[pairx_height:]
   210	
   211	        pairx_img = cv2.cvtColor(pairx_img, cv2.COLOR_BGR2RGB)
   212	        toReturn.append(pairx_img)
   213	    return toReturn
   214	
   215	class body(BaseModel):
   216	    # API input parameters
   217	    image1_uris: list[str]
   218	    bb1: list[list[float]]
   219	    theta1: list[float] = [0.0]
   220	    image2_uris: list[str]

     1	import logging
     2	import cv2
     3	import numpy as np
     4	from torchvision import transforms
     5	
     6	logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
     7	
     8	def unnormalize(img_base):
     9	    aug_mean = np.array([0.485, 0.456, 0.406])
    10	    aug_std = np.array([0.229, 0.224, 0.225])
    11	    unnormalize = transforms.Normalize((-aug_mean / aug_std).tolist(), (1.0 / aug_std).tolist())
    12	    img_unnorm = unnormalize(img_base)
    13	
    14	    return img_unnorm
    15	
    16	def resize_image(image, new_height):
    17	    aspect_ratio = image.shape[1] / image.shape[0]
    18	    new_width = int(new_height * aspect_ratio)
    19	    resized_image = cv2.resize(image, (new_width, new_height))
    20	    return resized_image
    21	
    22	## Functions for handling rotated bounding boxes
    23	
    24	def rotate_box(x1,y1,x2,y2,theta):
    25	    xm = (x1 + x2) // 2
    26	    ym = (y1 + y2) // 2
    27	
    28	    h = int(y2 - y1)
    29	    w = int(x2 - x1)
    30	
    31	    R = np.array([
    32	        [np.cos(theta), -np.sin(theta)],
    33	        [np.sin(theta), np.cos(theta)]
    34	    ])
    35	
    36	    A = np.array([[x1, y1], [x1, y2], [x2, y2], [x2, y1], [x1, y1]])
    37	    C = np.array([[xm, ym]])
    38	    RA = (A - C) @ R.T + C
    39	    RA = RA.astype(int)
    40	
    41	    return RA
    42	
    43	def crop_rect(img, rect):
    44	    center, size, angle = rect[0], rect[1], rect[2]
    45	    center, size = tuple(map(int, center)), tuple(map(int, size))
    46	
    47	    height, width = img.shape[0], img.shape[1]
    48	    
    49	    diag_len = int(np.sqrt(height * height + width * width))
    50	    new_width = diag_len
    51	    new_height = diag_len
    52	
    53	    blank_canvas = np.ones((new_height, new_width, 3), dtype=img.dtype) * 255
    54	
    55	    x_offset = (new_width - width) // 2
    56	    y_offset = (new_height - height) // 2
    57	
    58	    blank_canvas[y_offset:y_offset+height, x_offset:x_offset+width] = img
    59	
    60	    new_center_x = new_width // 2
    61	    new_center_y = new_height // 2
    62	
    63	    M = cv2.getRotationMatrix2D((new_center_x, new_center_y), np.rad2deg(angle), 1)
    64	
    65	    img_rot = cv2.warpAffine(blank_canvas, M, (new_width, new_height), flags=cv2.INTER_LINEAR, 
    66	                             borderMode=cv2.BORDER_CONSTANT, borderValue=(255,255,255))
    67	
    68	    new_center = np.dot(M[:,:2], np.array([center[0], center[1]]) + np.array([x_offset, y_offset])) + M[:,2]
    69	
    70	    img_crop = cv2.getRectSubPix(img_rot, size, new_center)
    71	    return img_crop, img_rot
    72	
    73	
    74	def get_chip_from_img(img, bbox, theta):
    75	    x1,y1,w,h = bbox
    76	    x2 = x1 + w
    77	    y2 = y1 + h
    78	    xm = (x1 + x2) // 2
    79	    ym = (y1 + y2) // 2
    80	
    81	    # Do a faster, regular crop if theta is negligible
    82	    if abs(theta) < 0.1:
    83	        x1, y1, w, h = [max(0, int(x)) for x in bbox]
    84	        cropped_image = img[y1 : y1 + h, x1 : x1 + w]
    85	    else:
    86	        cropped_image = crop_rect(img, ((xm, ym), (x2-x1, y2-y1), theta))[0]
    87	
    88	    if min(cropped_image.shape) < 1:
    89	        # Use original image
    90	        logger.warning(f'Using original image. Invalid parameters - theta: {theta}, bbox: {bbox}')
    91	        cropped_image = img
    92	
    93	    return cropped_image
    94	
    95	def load_image(image_path):
    96	    image = cv2.imread(image_path)
    97	    image = cv2.cvtColor(image, cv2.COLOR_BGR2RGB)
    98	    return image

     8	import torchvision.transforms as T
     9	from albumentations.core.transforms_interface import ImageOnlyTransform
    10	from PIL import Image
    11	import numpy as np
    12	
    13	class PyTorchResize(ImageOnlyTransform):
    14	    """Wrap PyTorch Resize transform for Albumentations compatibility."""
    15	    def __init__(self, height, width, interpolation=T.InterpolationMode.BILINEAR, always_apply=False, p=1.0):
    16	        super().__init__(always_apply, p)
    17	        self.resize = T.Resize(size=(height, width), interpolation=interpolation)
    18	
    19	    def apply(self, img, **params):
    20	        # Convert numpy array to PIL Image
    21	        img_pil = Image.fromarray(img)
    22	
    23	        # Apply the resize transform
    24	        img_pil_resized = self.resize(img_pil)
    25	
    26	        # Convert back to numpy array
    27	        return np.array(img_pil_resized)
    28	
    29	
    30	def triangle(img, p):
    31	    xx = numpy.random.rand(1)[0]
    32	    if xx > p:
    33	        h, w, _= img.shape
    34	        limitw = int(w * 0.3)
    35	        limith = int(h * 0.25)
    36	        desc = 0
    37	        step = limitw / limith
    38	        for i in range(limith):
    39	            img[i][:limitw - int(step * i)] = (255, 255, 255)
    40	    return img
    41	
    42	class Triangle(ImageOnlyTransform):
    43	    def __init__(self, p):
    44	        super(Triangle, self).__init__(p)
    45	        self.p = p
    46	    def apply(self, img , **params):
    47	        return triangle(img , self.p)
    48	
    49	def get_train_transforms(image_size):
    50	    return albumentations.Compose(
    51	        [   
    52	            Triangle(p=0.5),
    53	            PyTorchResize(image_size[0], image_size[1], always_apply=True),
    54	            albumentations.OneOf([
    55	                albumentations.Sharpen(p=0.3),
    56	                albumentations.ToGray(p=0.3),
    57	                albumentations.CLAHE(p=0.3),
    58	            ], p=0.5),
    59	            albumentations.ShiftScaleRotate(
    60	                shift_limit=0.25, scale_limit=0.2, rotate_limit=15, p=0.5
    61	            ),
    62	            albumentations.ColorJitter(brightness=0.1, contrast=0.1, saturation=0.1),
    63	            albumentations.Normalize(),
    64	            ToTensorV2(),
    65	        ]
    66	    )
    67	
    68	def get_valid_transforms(image_size):
    69	    return albumentations.Compose(
    70	        [
    71	            albumentations.Resize(image_size[0], image_size[1], always_apply=True),
    72	            albumentations.Normalize(),
    73	            ToTensorV2(p=1.0)
    74	        ]
    75	    )
    76

     1	import torch
     2	from tqdm import tqdm
     3	import cv2
     4	import torchvision.transforms as transforms
     5	from PIL import Image
     6	import numpy as np
     7	
     8	from .pairx.core import explain
     9	from .pairx.xai_dataset import get_pretransform_img
    10	from .helpers import get_chip_from_img, load_image
    11	
    12	
    13	def draw_one(
    14	    device,
    15	    test_loader,
    16	    model,
    17	    crop_bbox,
    18	    visualization_type="lines_and_colors",
    19	    layer_key="backbone.blocks.3",
    20	    k_lines=20,
    21	    k_colors=10,
    22	):
    23	    """
    24	    Generates a PAIR-X explanation for the provided images and model.
    25	
    26	    Args:
    27	        device (str or torch.device): Device to use (cuda or cpu).
    28	        test_loader (DataLoader): Should contain two images, with 4 items for each (image, name, path, bbox as xywh).
    29	        model (torch.nn.Module or equivalent): The deep metric learning model.
    30	        visualization_type (str): The part of the PAIR-X visualization to return, selected from "lines_and_colors" (default), "only_lines", and "only_colors".
    31	        layer_keys (str): The key of the intermediate layer to be used for explanation. Defaults to 'backbone.blocks.3'.
    32	        k_lines (int, optional): The number of matches to visualize as lines. Defaults to 20.
    33	        k_colors (int, optional): The number of matches to backpropagate to original image pixels. Defaults to 10.
    34	
    35	    Returns:
    36	        numpy.ndarray: PAIR-X visualization of type visualization_type.
    37	    """
    38	    assert test_loader.batch_size == 1, "test_loader should have a batch size of 1"
    39	    assert len(test_loader) == 2, "test_loader should only contain two images"
    40	    assert visualization_type in (
    41	        "lines_and_colors",
    42	        "only_lines",
    43	        "only_colors",
    44	    ), "unsupported visualization type"
    45	
    46	    transformed_images = []
    47	    pretransform_images = []
    48	
    49	    # get transformed and untransformed images out of test_loader
    50	    for batch in test_loader:
    51	        (transformed_image,), _, (path,), (bbox,), (theta,) = batch[:5]
    52	
    53	        if len(transformed_image.shape) == 3:
    54	            transformed_image = transformed_image.unsqueeze(0)
    55	
    56	        transformed_images.append(transformed_image.to(device))
    57	
    58	        img_size = tuple(transformed_image.shape[-2:])
    59	        pretransform_image = load_image(path)
    60	
    61	        if crop_bbox:
    62	            pretransform_image = get_chip_from_img(pretransform_image, bbox, theta)
    63	
    64	        pretransform_image = np.array(transforms.Resize(img_size)(Image.fromarray(pretransform_image)))
    65	        pretransform_images.append(pretransform_image)
    66	
    67	    img_0, img_1 = transformed_images
    68	    img_np_0, img_np_1 = pretransform_images
    69	
    70	    # If only returning image with lines, skip generating color maps to save time
    71	    if visualization_type == "only_lines":
    72	        k_colors = 0
    73	
    74	    # generate explanation image and return
    75	    model.eval()
    76	    model.device = device
    77	    pairx_img = explain(
    78	        img_0,
    79	        img_1,
    80	        img_np_0,
    81	        img_np_1,
    82	        model,
    83	        [layer_key],
    84	        k_lines=k_lines,
    85	        k_colors=k_colors,
    86	    )
    87	
    88	    pairx_height = pairx_img.shape[0] // 2
    89	
    90	    if visualization_type == "only_lines":
    91	        return pairx_img[:pairx_height]
    92	    elif visualization_type == "only_colors":
    93	        return pairx_img[pairx_height:]
    94	
    95	    pairx_img = cv2.cvtColor(pairx_img, cv2.COLOR_BGR2RGB)
    96	
    97	    return pairx_img
     1	import pandas as pd
     2	import os
     3	from PIL import Image, ImageOps
     4	import math
     5	import torchvision.transforms as transforms
     6	import numpy as np
     7	
     8	class XAIDataset:
     9	    def __init__(self, df, img_size=(440,440), img_transform=None, img_path=""):
    10	        assert isinstance(df, pd.DataFrame), "df must be a pandas DataFrame object"
    11	        for col in {"annot", "image", "name"}:
    12	            assert col in df.columns, f'df must contain column {col}'
    13	        if "x" in df.columns:
    14	            self.bbox = True
    15	            for col in {"x", "y", "w", "h"}:
    16	                assert col in df.columns, f'if using bounding boxes, df must contain column {col}'
    17	        else:
    18	            self.bbox = False
    19	
    20	        self.theta = "theta" in df.columns
    21	
    22	        self.df = df
    23	        self.img_size = img_size
    24	        self.img_transform = img_transform
    25	        self.img_path = img_path
    26	    
    27	    def _load_image(self, row, transform=True):
    28	        annot = row["annot"]
    29	        img_path = os.path.join(self.img_path, row["image"])
    30	        name = row["name"]   
    31	
    32	        with open(img_path, "rb") as f:
    33	            img = ImageOps.exif_transpose(Image.open(f))
    34	            img.load()
    35	
    36	        if self.bbox:
    37	            x, y, w, h = row["x"], row["y"], row["w"], row["h"]
    38	            if w <= 1:
    39	                x = x * img.width
    40	                y = y * img.height
    41	                w = w * img.width
    42	                h = h * img.height
    43	                
    44	            img = img.crop((x, y, min(x + w, img.width), min(y + h, img.height)))
    45	        if self.theta:
    46	            img = img.rotate(math.degrees(row["theta"]))
    47	            
    48	        img = transforms.Resize(self.img_size)(img)
    49	
    50	        if transform and self.img_transform:
    51	            return self.img_transform(img), name, annot
    52	
    53	        return np.array(img), name, annot
    54	
    55	
    56	    def __len__(self):
    57	        return len(self.df)
    58	        
    59	    def __getitem__(self, idx):
    60	        return self._load_image(self.df.iloc[idx])
    61	
    62	    def get_image_pretransform(self, annot_id):
    63	        selected_row = self.df[self.df["annot"] == annot_id]
    64	        assert len(selected_row) == 1, f'{len(selected_row)} rows found in df with annot={annot_id}'
    65	        return self._load_image(selected_row.iloc[0], transform=False)
    66	
    67	    def get_image_transformed(self, annot_id):
    68	        selected_row = self.df[self.df["annot"] == annot_id]
    69	        assert len(selected_row) == 1, f'{len(selected_row)} rows found in df with annot={annot_id}'
    70	        return self._load_image(selected_row.iloc[0])
    71	
    72	    def save_df(self, output_dir):
    73	        self.df.to_csv(os.path.join(output_dir, 'df.csv'), index=False)
    74	    
    75	    def get_img_pair(self, device, annot_0, annot_1):
    76	        img_0, _, _ = self.get_image_transformed(annot_0)
    77	        img_1, _, _ = self.get_image_transformed(annot_1)
    78	
    79	        img_0 = img_0.unsqueeze(0).to(device)
    80	        img_1 = img_1.unsqueeze(0).to(device)
    81	
    82	        img_np_0, _, _ = self.get_image_pretransform(annot_0)
    83	        img_np_1, _, _ = self.get_image_pretransform(annot_1)
    84	
    85	        return img_0, img_1, img_np_0, img_np_1
    86	
    87	def get_img_pair_from_paths(device, img_path_0, img_path_1, img_size, img_transform):
    88	    def get_img_pair_from_path(img_path, transform):
    89	        with open(img_path, "rb") as f:
    90	            img = ImageOps.exif_transpose(Image.open(f))
    91	            img.load()
    92	
    93	            img = transforms.Resize(img_size)(img)
    94	
    95	            if transform:
    96	                return img_transform(img).unsqueeze(0).to(device)
    97	
    98	            return np.array(img)
    99	    
   100	    return (get_img_pair_from_path(img_path_0, transform=True),
   101	            get_img_pair_from_path(img_path_1, transform=True),
   102	            get_img_pair_from_path(img_path_0, transform=False),
   103	            get_img_pair_from_path(img_path_1, transform=False),)
   104	
   105	def get_pretransform_img(img_path, img_size, bbox=None):
   106	    with open(img_path, "rb") as f:
   107	        img = ImageOps.exif_transpose(Image.open(f))
   108	        img.load()
   109	
   110	    if bbox is not None:
   111	        x, y, w, h = bbox
   112	        if w <= 1:
   113	            x = x * img.width
   114	            y = y * img.height
   115	            w = w * img.width
   116	            h = h * img.height
   117	
   118	        x, y, w, h = (int(val) for val in (x, y, w, h))
   119	            
   120	        img = img.crop((x, y, min(x + w, img.width), min(y + h, img.height)))
   121	    
   122	    img = transforms.Resize(img_size)(img)
   123	
   124	    return np.array(img)

     1	## Functions for handling rotated bounding boxes
     2	
     3	import numpy as np
     4	from PIL import Image as PILImage
     5	import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
     6	
     7	
     8	def load_image(image_path):
     9	    image = np.array(PILImage.open(image_path).convert('RGB'))
    10	    return image
    11	
    12	def imshow(img):
    13	    plt.figure(figsize=(12, 8))
    14	    plt_img = img.copy()
    15	    plt.imshow(plt_img)
    16	    plt.show()
    17	
    18	def show_image(image_path):
    19	    image = load_image(image_path)
    20	    imshow(image)
    21	
    22	def rotate_box(x1,y1,x2,y2,theta):
    23	    xm = (x1 + x2) // 2
    24	    ym = (y1 + y2) // 2
    25	
    26	    h = int(y2 - y1)
    27	    w = int(x2 - x1)
    28	
    29	    R = np.array([
    30	        [np.cos(theta), -np.sin(theta)],
    31	        [np.sin(theta), np.cos(theta)]
    32	    ])
    33	
    34	    A = np.array([[x1, y1], [x1, y2], [x2, y2], [x2, y1], [x1, y1]])
    35	    C = np.array([[xm, ym]])
    36	    RA = (A - C) @ R.T + C
    37	    RA = RA.astype(int)
    38	
    39	    return RA
    40	
    41	def crop_rect(img, rect):
    42	    """Crop a rotated rectangle from an image using PIL (no OpenCV)."""
    43	    center, size, angle = rect[0], rect[1], rect[2]
    44	    center, size = tuple(map(int, center)), tuple(map(int, size))
    45	
    46	    height, width = img.shape[0], img.shape[1]
    47	
    48	    diag_len = int(np.sqrt(height * height + width * width))
    49	    new_width = diag_len
    50	    new_height = diag_len
    51	
    52	    # Create white canvas and paste image centered
    53	    blank_canvas = np.ones((new_height, new_width, 3), dtype=img.dtype) * 255
    54	
    55	    x_offset = (new_width - width) // 2
    56	    y_offset = (new_height - height) // 2
    57	
    58	    blank_canvas[y_offset:y_offset+height, x_offset:x_offset+width] = img
    59	
    60	    # Convert to PIL for rotation
    61	    pil_canvas = PILImage.fromarray(blank_canvas)
    62	
    63	    # PIL rotate uses degrees, counter-clockwise positive (same as cv2.getRotationMatrix2D)
    64	    angle_deg = np.rad2deg(angle)
    65	    new_center_x = new_width // 2
    66	    new_center_y = new_height // 2
    67	
    68	    # Rotate around center of canvas
    69	    pil_rotated = pil_canvas.rotate(angle_deg, resample=PILImage.BILINEAR, center=(new_center_x, new_center_y), fillcolor=(255, 255, 255))
    70	
    71	    img_rot = np.array(pil_rotated)
    72	
    73	    # Compute where the crop center moved to after rotation
    74	    cos_a = np.cos(np.deg2rad(angle_deg))
    75	    sin_a = np.sin(np.deg2rad(angle_deg))
    76	    # Point relative to rotation center
    77	    px = center[0] + x_offset - new_center_x
    78	    py = center[1] + y_offset - new_center_y
    79	    # Apply rotation (counter-clockwise)
    80	    new_cx = cos_a * px + sin_a * py + new_center_x
    81	    new_cy = -sin_a * px + cos_a * py + new_center_y
    82	
    83	    # Crop sub-rectangle centered at (new_cx, new_cy) with given size
    84	    crop_w, crop_h = size
    85	    x1 = int(new_cx - crop_w / 2)
    86	    y1 = int(new_cy - crop_h / 2)
    87	    x2 = x1 + crop_w
    88	    y2 = y1 + crop_h
    89	
    90	    # Clamp to image bounds
    91	    x1c = max(0, x1)
    92	    y1c = max(0, y1)
    93	    x2c = min(new_width, x2)
    94	    y2c = min(new_height, y2)
    95	
    96	    img_crop = img_rot[y1c:y2c, x1c:x2c]
    97	
    98	    # Pad if crop extends beyond canvas
    99	    if img_crop.shape[0] != crop_h or img_crop.shape[1] != crop_w:
   100	        padded = np.ones((crop_h, crop_w, 3), dtype=img.dtype) * 255
   101	        paste_x = x1c - x1
   102	        paste_y = y1c - y1
   103	        padded[paste_y:paste_y+img_crop.shape[0], paste_x:paste_x+img_crop.shape[1]] = img_crop
   104	        img_crop = padded
   105	
   106	    return img_crop, img_rot
   107	
   108	
   109	def get_chip_from_img(img, bbox, theta):
   110	    x1,y1,w,h = bbox
   111	    x2 = x1 + w
   112	    y2 = y1 + h
   113	    xm = (x1 + x2) // 2
   114	    ym = (y1 + y2) // 2
   115	
   116	    # Treat NaN/None/invalid theta as zero rotation
   117	    try:
   118	        theta_valid = float(theta)
   119	        if theta_valid != theta_valid:  # NaN check
   120	            theta_valid = 0
   121	    except (TypeError, ValueError):
   122	        theta_valid = 0
   123	    theta = theta_valid
   124	
   125	    # Do a faster, regular crop if theta is negligible
   126	    if abs(theta) < 0.1:
   127	        x1, y1, w, h = [max(0, int(x)) for x in bbox]
   128	        cropped_image = img[y1 : y1 + h, x1 : x1 + w]
   129	    else:
   130	        cropped_image = crop_rect(img, ((xm, ym), (x2-x1, y2-y1), theta))[0]
   131	
   132	    if min(cropped_image.shape) < 1:
   133	        # Use original image
   134	        print(f'Using original image. Invalid parameters - theta: {theta}, bbox: {bbox}')
   135	        cropped_image = img
   136	
   137	    return cropped_image

     8	# Mapping of model types to their respective module and class names
     9	MODEL_REGISTRY = {
    10	    'yolo-ultralytics': {
    11	        'module': 'app.models.yolo_ultralytics',
    12	        'class': 'YOLOUltralyticsModel'
    13	    },
    14	    'megadetector': {
    15	        'module': 'app.models.megadetector',
    16	        'class': 'MegaDetectorModel',
    17	    },
    18	    'miewid': {
    19	        'module': 'app.models.miewid',

    21	    },

    25	    },

    29	    },
    30	    'densenet-classifier': {
    31	        'module': 'app.models.densenet_classifier',
    32	        'class': 'DenseNetClassifierModel'
    33	    },
    34	    'lightnet': {
    35	        'module': 'app.models.lightnet_model',
    36	        'class': 'LightNetModel'
    37	    }
    38	    # Add new model types here as they are implemented
    39	}
    40	
    41	class ModelHandler:
    42	    """Handler class for managing multiple model instances.
    43	    
    44	    This class provides a unified interface to load and access different types of models.
    45	    It maintains a registry of available model types and their implementations.
    46	    """
    47	    
    48	    def __init__(self):
    49	        """Initialize the ModelHandler with an empty models dictionary."""
    50	        self.models = {}
    51	    
    52	    def load_model(self, model_id: str, model_type: str, model_path: str = "", 
    53	                  device: str = 'cpu', **kwargs) -> None:
    54	        """Load a model with the specified parameters.
    55	        
    56	        Args:
    57	            model_id: Unique identifier for the model
    58	            model_type: Type of the model (must be registered in MODEL_REGISTRY)
    59	            model_path: Path to the model file or model identifier
    60	            device: Device to load the model on (e.g., 'cpu', 'cuda')
    61	            **kwargs: Additional model-specific parameters
    62	            
    63	        Raises:
    64	            ValueError: If the model type is not supported or if there's an error loading the model
    65	        """
    66	        if model_type not in MODEL_REGISTRY:
    67	            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported model type: {model_type}. "
    68	                           f"Available types: {list(MODEL_REGISTRY.keys())}")
    69	        
    70	        try:
    71	            # Dynamically import the model class
    72	            model_info = MODEL_REGISTRY[model_type]
    73	            module = importlib.import_module(model_info['module'])
    74	            model_class = getattr(module, model_info['class'])
    75	            
    76	            # Create and initialize the model
    77	            model_instance: BaseModel = model_class()
    78	            model_instance.load(model_path=model_path, device=device, model_id=model_id, **kwargs)
    79	            
    80	            # Store the model instance
    81	            self.models[model_id] = {
    82	                'instance': model_instance,
    83	                'type': model_type,
    84	                'config': {
    85	                    'model_path': model_path,
    86	                    'device': device,
    87	                    **kwargs
    88	                }
    89	            }
    90	            
    91	            logger.info(f"Successfully loaded model '{model_id}' of type '{model_type}'")
    92	            
    93	        except Exception as e:
    94	            logger.error(f"Error loading model '{model_id}': {str(e)}")
    95	            raise ValueError(f"Failed to load model '{model_id}': {str(e)}")
    96	    
    97	    def get_model(self, model_id: str) -> Optional[BaseModel]:
    98	        """Get a loaded model by its ID.
    99	        
   100	        Args:
   101	            model_id: ID of the model to retrieve
   102	            
   103	        Returns:
   104	            The model instance if found, None otherwise
   105	        """
   106	        return self.models.get(model_id, {}).get('instance')
   107	    
   108	    def predict(self, model_id: str, image_bytes: bytes, **kwargs) -> Dict[str, Any]:
   109	        """Run inference using the specified model.
   110	        
   111	        Args:
   112	            model_id: ID of the model to use for prediction
   113	            image_bytes: Image data as bytes
   114	            **kwargs: Additional inference parameters
   115	            
   116	        Returns:
   117	            Dictionary containing the prediction results
   118	            
   119	        Raises:
   120	            ValueError: If the model is not found
   121	        """
   122	        model_info = self.models.get(model_id)
   123	        if not model_info:
   124	            raise ValueError(f"Model with ID '{model_id}' not found")
   125	            
   126	        return model_info['instance'].predict(image_bytes, **kwargs)
   127	    
   128	    def get_model_info(self, model_id: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
   129	        """Get information about a loaded model.
   130	        
   131	        Args:
   132	            model_id: ID of the model
   133	            
   134	        Returns:
   135	            Dictionary containing model information
   136	            
   137	        Raises:
   138	            ValueError: If the model is not found
   139	        """
   140	        model_info = self.models.get(model_id)
   141	        if not model_info:
   142	            raise ValueError(f"Model with ID '{model_id}' not found")
   143	            
   144	        return {
   145	            'model_id': model_id,
   146	            'model_type': model_info['type'],
   147	            'config': model_info['config'],
   148	            'info': model_info['instance'].get_model_info()
   149	        }
   150	    
   151	    def list_models(self) -> Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]]:
   152	        """Get information about all loaded models.
   153	        
   154	        Returns:
   155	            Dictionary mapping model IDs to their information
   156	        """
   157	        return {
   158	            model_id: self.get_model_info(model_id)
   159	            for model_id in self.models
   160	        }

**Findings**
No correctness findings in the reviewed scope. The extraction and PairX preprocessing changes are aligned with WBIA’s valid/test transform path.

**Answers**
1. Yes. [miewid.py](/mnt/c/ml-service/app/models/miewid.py:99) matches WBIA’s [transforms.py](/mnt/c/wbia-plugin-miew-id/wbia_miew_id/datasets/transforms.py:68): `Resize -> Normalize -> ToTensorV2`. Omitting `always_apply=True` and `p=1.0` is semantically equivalent here because the defaults are already always-on.
2. No concern. `Image.open(...).convert("RGB")` followed by `np.array(...)` is a lossless boundary conversion to HWC RGB `uint8`, which is what albumentations expects.
3. Correct. [explain_router.py](/mnt/c/ml-service/app/routers/explain_router.py:120) feeds a numpy RGB chip into `preprocess`; removing `Image.fromarray(...)` is appropriate for albumentations.
4. Leaving `torchvision.transforms` in [explain_router.py](/mnt/c/ml-service/app/routers/explain_router.py:127) is fine. That resize is display/pretransform visualization plumbing and mirrors WBIA’s PairX draw path, not model input preprocessing.
5. Yes. `ToTensorV2()` defaults to `p=1.0`.
6. Only minor cleanup: the comment in [miewid.py](/mnt/c/ml-service/app/models/miewid.py:219) references a stale line number. Not a behavioral issue. Also, if you later make `IMAGE_SIZE` non-square, treat it consistently as `(height, width)` because that is albumentations’ argument order.

49,350
**Findings**
No correctness findings in the reviewed scope. The extraction and PairX preprocessing changes are aligned with WBIA’s valid/test transform path.

**Answers**
1. Yes. [miewid.py](/mnt/c/ml-service/app/models/miewid.py:99) matches WBIA’s [transforms.py](/mnt/c/wbia-plugin-miew-id/wbia_miew_id/datasets/transforms.py:68): `Resize -> Normalize -> ToTensorV2`. Omitting `always_apply=True` and `p=1.0` is semantically equivalent here because the defaults are already always-on.
2. No concern. `Image.open(...).convert("RGB")` followed by `np.array(...)` is a lossless boundary conversion to HWC RGB `uint8`, which is what albumentations expects.
3. Correct. [explain_router.py](/mnt/c/ml-service/app/routers/explain_router.py:120) feeds a numpy RGB chip into `preprocess`; removing `Image.fromarray(...)` is appropriate for albumentations.
4. Leaving `torchvision.transforms` in [explain_router.py](/mnt/c/ml-service/app/routers/explain_router.py:127) is fine. That resize is display/pretransform visualization plumbing and mirrors WBIA’s PairX draw path, not model input preprocessing.
5. Yes. `ToTensorV2()` defaults to `p=1.0`.
6. Only minor cleanup: the comment in [miewid.py](/mnt/c/ml-service/app/models/miewid.py:219) references a stale line number. Not a behavioral issue. Also, if you later make `IMAGE_SIZE` non-square, treat it consistently as `(height, width)` because that is albumentations’ argument order.
